requires v1.MutatingWebhook, but got %T\", hook)\n   144→\t\t}\n   145→\t\t// This means that during reinvocation, a webhook will not be\n   146→\t\t// called for the first time. 190→\t\t\tadmissionmetrics.Metrics.ObserveWebhook(ctx, hook.Name, time.Since(t), rejected, versionedAttr.Attributes, \"admit\", 200)\n   191→\t\t}\n   192→\t\tif changed {\n   193→\t\t\t// Patch had changed the object. Prepare to reinvoke all previous mutations that are eligible for re-invocation.\n   194→\t\t\twebhookReinvokeCtx.RequireReinvokingPreviouslyInvokedPlugins()\n 198→\t\t\twebhookReinvokeCtx.AddReinvocableWebhookToPreviouslyInvoked(invocation.Webhook.GetUID())\n   199→\t\t}\n   200→\t\tif err == nil {\n   201→\t\t\tcontinue\n   202→\t\t}\n   203→\n 218→\t\t\t\t\t// parent context is canceled or timed out, no point in continuing\n   219→\t\t\t\t\treturn apierrors.NewTimeoutError(\"request did not complete within requested timeout\", 0)\n   220→\t\t\t\tdefault:\n   221→\t\t\t\t\t// individual webhook timed out, but parent context did not, continue\n   222→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   223→\t\t\t\t}\n   224→\t\t\t}\n Both plugins inherit from the generic Webhook base class (generic/webhook.go) which provides the common infrastructure for webhook processing. The generic Webhook dispatcher interface (generic/interfaces.go) defines the Dispatcher interface that is implemented differently for mutating and validating webhooks. The dispatcher calls the callAttrMutatingHook method for each webhook, which applies JSON patches to the object. For validating webhooks, the validatingDispatcher (validating/dispatcher.go) implements parallel dispatch using goroutines and a WaitGroup, allowing multiple webhooks to be called concurrently while still collecting any validation errors. The WebhookAccessor abstraction (accessors.go) provides a unified interface to both MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook types, with separate implementations for each (mutatingWebhookAccessor and validatingWebhookAccessor). This accessor pattern abstracts differences between the webhook types while providing common methods for getting configuration, client connections, and compiled match conditions. The webhook configurations are managed by the mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager, which act as Source implementations providing lists of WebhookAccessor objects. The API types MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration (admissionregistration/v1/types.go) define the Kubernetes resource types that store webhook configurations, with each containing lists of MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook objects respectively. implements a generic framework for both mutating and validating webhooks. The chain starts with two main plugins registered in the admission system: MutatingAdmissionWebhook (mutating/plugin.go) and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook (validating/plugin.go). Both plugins inherit from the generic Webhook base class (generic/webhook.go) which provides the common infrastructure for webhook processing. The generic Webhook dispatcher interface (generic/interfaces.go) defines the Dispatcher interface that is implemented differently for mutating and validating webhooks. For mutating webhooks, the mutatingDispatcher (mutating/dispatcher.go) processes webhooks sequentially while implementing reinvocation logic via the webhookReinvokeContext (mutating/reinvocationcontext.go). This allows webhooks marked with IfNeededReinvocationPolicy to be called again if earlier mutations changed the object. The dispatcher calls the callAttrMutatingHook method for each webhook, which applies JSON patches to the object. For validating webhooks, the validatingDispatcher (validating/dispatcher.go) implements parallel dispatch using goroutines and a WaitGroup, allowing multiple webhooks to be called concurrently while still collecting any validation errors. The WebhookAccessor abstraction (accessors.go) provides a unified interface to both MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook types, with separate implementations for each (mutatingWebhookAccessor and validatingWebhookAccessor). This accessor pattern abstracts differences between the webhook types while providing common methods for getting configuration, client connections, and compiled match conditions. The webhook configurations are managed by the mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager and validatingWebhookConfigurationManager, which act as Source implementations providing lists of WebhookAccessor objects. The API types MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration (admissionregistration/v1/types.go) define the Kubernetes resource types that store webhook configurations, with each containing lists of MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook objects respectively. The processing chain ensures that admission requests are evaluated against all registered webhooks with proper error handling (Fail vs Ignore failure policies), timeout enforcement, and audit annotation recording.\"\n    56→}\n    57→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
